11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，截至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日共 收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3533</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">9</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">九年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">九年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">110</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整九年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">六万字</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">42</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">39</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">42</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1656</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk159649535"></a><a name="_Hlk162449568"></a><a name="_Hlk175727158"></a><a name="_Hlk181147271"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181147271;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181147271;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183670217"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈海霞</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东法轮功学员。广东雷州市白沙镇梛楠村人，后在湛江霞山区租住，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月末，在雷州市向民众发放法轮功资料的时候，被告，遭关押了几天后，获释，回到自己租住的房子。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月初，陈海霞又被警察绑架、抄家。后遭判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在血压高不适合关押的情况下，中院维持冤判，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被关押到广州女子监狱迫害。目前，陈海霞被洗脑灌输、野蛮灌食，眼睛赤红、非常憔悴，仅一个月余，其境况令家人十分担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈气：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，福建省福州市人，福州市鼓楼区洪山镇凤湖小区<span lang="EN-US">60</span>号公民，强拆受害者，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。早年，因自家房屋曾遭政府强拆，不安置、不赔偿，遂被迫多年赴京上访讨说法，但问题却一直得不到解决，反而成为当地各级政府的维稳对象，屡遭福州市当局围追堵截和非法拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因与其他访民在福州市中心的五一广场诉冤，而被鼓楼区安泰派出所警方抓走，并被关押在福州市公安局禁毒大队院内；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，又因和多名维权民众前往美国驻华大使馆寻求救助，而曾被福建省驻京维稳人员强行遣返原籍；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因福州市洪山镇民众屡遭当局派出的警方、城管以及雇佣的黑社会成员实施暴力逼迁，故其等被强拆受害者自发在洪山镇凤池新村推棺材维权，以示誓死捍卫家园的决心；此举虽鼓舞了民众维权勇气，但却触及到福州市当局管理者的敏感神经，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天之后的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被福州市鼓楼区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，并送福州市第一看守所关押，后又被转到第二看守所续押；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，才被准予取保候审；但不久，又因此次在福建省政府、福建省高级法院门外和福州市五一广场等场所举牌维权，而于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被当地警方收监逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被福州市罗源县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；刑满出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾因和众多维权访民集体前去迎接维权人士严兴声出狱，放鞭炮以示庆祝，故又被福州市警方拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾因与同是维权访民的陈芳、江心等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人进京继续信访投诉，而在北京暂住的酒店附近突遭<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名政府指派的黑保安围追堵截，后被野蛮截访送回原籍，且途中遭到非人道折磨和虐待；到达原籍后又被转交给另一伙恶势力团伙，任由他们将其等人非法拘禁在当地附近山沟里的一户人家，直到同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，才被扔在福州市新店镇的森林公园某山脚下；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因中共两会期间进京上访，而被福州市当局以“寻衅滋事”为由拘禁在当地一黑监狱内，因其无法忍受看押人员对其的极端折磨和虐待，就爬到已拆除的窗户上而被路人看见，遂被报警并将现场视频发到网上，引起网民强烈关注，故而其再次被福州市鼓楼区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被福州市鼓楼区检察院以同罪名予以正式批捕和被很快起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其案在福州市鼓楼区法院开庭审理；虽当前福州市并无疫情，属低风险地区，但鼓楼区法院仍以疫情防控为由只允许其年迈老母和其女儿进入法院，观看远程视频开庭，另有其亲族成员以及多名福州维权公民前往围观和声援，但都被拦于法庭之外。目前被羁押于福州市鼓楼区看守所（又称福建省第二看守所，福建省福州市鼓楼区梅峰路<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">350000</span>）。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2022</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被鼓楼法院以寻衅滋事罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省青岛市城阳区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，女，家住青岛市城阳区惜福镇街道惜福镇小学校附近。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，城阳区公安分局闯入陈艳红家中将她强制抓捕到上马派出所，后警察抄家，将。她被抓捕的原因是她在发法轮功资料时，遭到不明真相的人恶意举报。陈艳红被抓捕后，一直在即墨普东看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被视频开庭、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被从即墨普东看守所转到山东省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">4/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b 11.0pt;">达日（藏）：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，他与赞查（藏）二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183670412"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜艳红</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，杜艳红去同修家时被警察抓捕，警察从她背包里搜出了内存卡、法轮功粘贴，当天对其抄家。后杜艳红被取保候审，强制罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份，法院开庭，杜艳红做了无罪辩护，杜艳红当天回家。后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份的一天下午，宁河区芦台镇派出所警察去杜艳红家，让她去派出所一趟办完事就回家，结果杜艳红一去不归，被关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，家人这才知道杜艳红被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，关押到天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183670457"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯蕴青</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉法轮功学员。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被绑架，关押在武汉东西湖区武汉第一看守所。参与绑架和扣押的部门有：武汉市网监支队，武汉市“国保”支队，江岸区公安分局后湖派出所。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，冯蕴青不服判决，上诉到武汉市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月武汉中级法院二审维持原判。现在冯蕴青被非法关押在武汉女子监狱（位于武汉市宝丰路）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">7/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">高明洁：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东淄博市博山区法轮功学员。法轮功学员王忠实、高明洁于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被抓捕、构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑：王忠实获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，被勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；高明洁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万。二人上诉，被中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B7%84%E5%8D%9A%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%A0%E5%AE%9E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-431828.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B7%84%E5%8D%9A%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%A0%E5%AE%9E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-431828.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">耿家峰：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1973</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，山东省沂水县籍人，山东省淄博市桓台县马桥镇辛庄村村民，维权访民，实名举报人，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，就开始因所在村落官员严重贪腐问题而实名举报维权，随被山东省桓台县当局视为需要打压的异己和维稳对象；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因先后三次上访投诉，被恒台县警方以“非正常上访”为由给予严厉警告；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，曾两次被恒台县警方以“非正常上访，扰乱公共场所秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，又被以警方“故意损害财物”、“扬言实施放火，非法携带管制刀具”为由分别处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，曾因所在辛庄村村主任郭世勋从金城石化公司往辛庄村的西北角运输化工废渣，污染土地，而向山东省各级环保部门举报，无果后，又于次日欲往北京环保部举报，随被县政府派人拦截并遭人毒打住院；过后其虽多次继续举报违法排污的村主任郭世勋，并要求警方尽快查处打人事件和为其被殴打导致常年半头痛后遗症做鉴定，但都被拒绝；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其再次被恒台县警方抓捕刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，并被要求退赔相关经济损失<span lang="EN-US">2803</span>元。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因桓台县田庄镇文庄村的维权人士张岗遭抓捕，张岗之妹向其求助，其为营救张岗，遂不惧险境，多次向各级主管部门及新闻媒体举报、控诉恒台县公安局非法拘禁人，从而引社会热议；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因维权者张岗已被批捕，其受张岗妹妹之托，立刻在微信群频繁发“紧急关注”，以呼吁更多正义人士关注张岗被捕事件；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，再次为声援张岗被抓事件而在新浪微博网站发文，揭露张岗所在田庄镇文庄村村委主任组织黑社会，贪污受贿、公账私存、挪用公款等渎职行为，因此文被人关注、转发近千次，遂立遭恒台县当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被恒台县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等再次刑拘，随后又被恒台县检察院很快以多项罪由正式批捕，并关押于桓台县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被淄博市恒台县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月）、“妨碍公务罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月）、“敲诈勒索罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月）三罪，数罪并罚决定执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被山东省淄博市中级法院二审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US"> 2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。目前疑似在山东省淄博监狱（又称山东省第四监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/46.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/46.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">9/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何丽霞：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江大庆市杜蒙县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共疯狂发动了对法轮功的迫害，何丽霞因讲法轮功真相，曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被中共劳教，有<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被迫害差点失去生命。这场迫害给何丽霞造成家庭破裂，幼小的女儿在失去妈妈的痛苦中长大。何丽霞迫流离失所近两年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月回家才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月左右，再<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被恶警抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日何丽霞再次被抓捕，关押在大庆市第二看守所。当天，大庆市、区、县有<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多名法轮功学员被抓捕，多数被抄家，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>来人被送进大庆市看守所关押，十多人被送拘留所关押。何丽霞在看守所绝食抗议关押迫害，<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后出现生命危险，国保警察找家人签字，办了“取保候审”。几天后，国保又找何丽霞，要所谓“走法律程序”，图谋对她判刑迫害。何丽霞被迫流离失所两年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，何丽霞在回家刚<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月，再次被恶警抓捕，被关押在杜蒙县看守所，后关押到大庆看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份，何丽霞被大庆市让胡路法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现关押到哈尔滨女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/26/2021-9-26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/26/2021-9-26.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贾建怀：</span></b></span></span></span><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃省兰州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月因发送真相资料被警察抓捕，后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，团结新村派出所警察以取手机为名，骗贾建怀到派出所后将他抓捕、刑事拘留，关押在兰州市红古区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日对他批捕，将他转关到西果园的兰州市第三看守所。在看守所恶劣的环境中，贾建怀出现高血压症状，高压有时在<span lang="EN-US">160</span>～<span lang="EN-US">180</span>，被迫一天吃两次药。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，锦州市公安局太和分局国保大队共抓捕了十几名法轮功学员，包括：张英玲（<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁）、金晓梅（<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁）、康桂云（<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁）、刘玉荣（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、李淑芳（<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁）、陈文学（<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁），都是老太太。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日获悉，辽宁省锦州市凌海市法院对这名老人下达判决，其中张英玲、金晓梅都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；康桂云<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；刘玉荣、李淑芳、陈文学皆被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金两千元。金晓梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b lang="EN-US">14000</span>元现金及很多个人物品，并把白宝华抓捕。其中这<span lang="EN-US">14000</span>元是白宝华用来给儿子治大腿血栓从亲戚朋友处借来的钱，都被抢去说成是用来做法轮功资料。随后，白宝华被送至元宝山区看守所关押。后白宝华被赤峰中级法院宣判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李保兰、齐文伯在发放法轮功资料时被豆张庄镇派出所警察抓捕并抄家。由于身体原因（血压高），她们被以取保候审的名义放回家中。但<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多来，公检法相关人员一直在构陷她们。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在家中被警察抓捕、抄家。当地公安、检察院以涉嫌所谓“破坏法律实施”的罪名将她刑事拘留，并将构陷材料递交到向阳区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日佳木斯市向阳区法院对此开庭，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。收到判决书后，刘金萍委托亲友辩护人上诉。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，佳木斯市中院违反法律程序，剥夺亲友辩护人的权利，没有公开开庭审理就做出了驳回上诉、维持原判的终审裁定。目前刘金萍被关押在佳木斯市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">潘玉峰：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁朝阳市两法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，潘玉峰在家中被北塔分局警察抓捕。潘玉峰是位难得的孝子，家中老母亲患老年痴呆，生活不能自理，一直由潘玉峰照顾。自潘玉峰被绑架后，老人无人照顾，很快消瘦了很多，在潘玉峰绑架近一年后老人悲苦离开人世，临终都未见到儿子一面。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，潘玉峰案开庭，律师做无罪辩护。后得知潘玉峰被双塔法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">23/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如凯•<a name="_Hlk183671314">嘎玛桑珠（藏）</a>：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1968</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，西藏自治区贡觉县人，藏族，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年度“西藏自治区劳动模范”，原嘎玛国际生态文化发展有限公司董事长、西藏天珠之路文化传播有限公司董事长、青海三江源生态环保发展有限公司董事长、东方收藏家协会和自然之友会员等，著名古董商，慈善家，环保人士，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其致力于文化与环境保护工作，曾多次获得政府颁发的相关奖项；曾为家乡建桥梁修学校、抚恤孤寡老人；曾成立著名的三江源生态环境保护协会，并从事文物收藏保护；曾创建天珠之路文化传播有限公司，并多次与省级博物馆进行合作；曾与中国藏学研究中心达成协议，准备将<span lang="EN-US">200</span>件珍藏的文物捐献给国家等等，被央视电台提名为<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年度慈善家；本为模范中国公民，之后却因得罪地方当局而备受牢狱之灾。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年，因其在不知情的前提下购买了总值为<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>美金的七世纪古董毯、刺绣枕垫与鞋子等被盗古墓物品，随被巴州警方以涉嫌“倒卖文物罪”于同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日刑拘，后经查证其对被窃之物确系毫不知情，且其拥有正规的买卖古董许可证，遂于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又因同一罪名被拘，之后又以同一理由于同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被正式解除取保候审。但十年之后旧事重提，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，第三次因涉嫌“倒卖文物罪”被西藏自治区若羌县警方刑拘，被关押在新疆维吾尔族自治区焉耆回族自治县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区焉耆回族自治县法院以“盗掘古墓葬罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元。现在新疆阿克苏地区的沙雅监狱服刑；据悉，在审讯期间曾多次遭遇酷刑，致其左耳几近失聪，双目视力模糊。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/1520241119.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/1520241119.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">24/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183671374"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王红霞</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，四川省资阳市安岳县人，绰号小莲、小梅、小吴、莲姐，安岳县安岳镇铁峰路<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号居民，前安岳县教师进修学校英语教师，茶叶生意经营者，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信徒，中国在押良心犯。因信仰和长期锻炼、宣传法轮功屡遭四川当局的逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，曾因锻炼法轮功而被资阳市当局以“利用邪教组织扰乱社会秩序”罪由分别劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年（三次共计<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年半），劳教期间曾屡遭酷刑折磨；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因外省法轮功友人到成都做茶叶经销考察，当与其会面时被突然出现的成都市便衣警察以“是吸毒犯”为借口强行带走，并先后送到新津洗脑班、二娥湖洗脑班关押；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被资阳市安岳县警方以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”予以逮捕，并关押于资阳市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被四川省资阳市简阳县法院以同罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年；其不服提出上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经四川省资阳市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月；据悉，曾在狱中因绝食抗议而致身体枯瘦如柴，生命垂危；其家属探监权（含约见律师）等遭禁。目前在四川省成都女子监狱六监区服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">25/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183671429"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王楣泓</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">:</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省牡丹江市法轮功学员，牡丹江市地质勘察所高级工程师，丈夫于宗海是画家，就职于牡丹江市图书馆。夫妻俩因修炼法轮功曾被判十多年。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，王楣泓被牡丹江市爱民区中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害，曾多次遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年获释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日又被哈尔滨市南岗区公安分局哈西派出所警察抓捕构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院庭审。后获悉，王楣泓被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初投入黑龙江女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/24/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437195.html<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">26/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183671469"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴旭钦</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员吴旭钦<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">27/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">夏霖：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US"> 9</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 15</span>日出生，贵州省人，北京市华一律师事务所合伙人，维权律师。曾因为人公义正派、代理案件认真有效而在业界有较高知名度；近年来，曾代理过包括艾未未、冉云飞等案在内的多起敏感维权案件；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾为北京市小贩崔英杰杀死城管李志强案做免费辩护律师；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾为刺死官员女服务员邓玉娇涉嫌故意杀人案做代理律师；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾与人权律师浦志强一起为地震义工谭作人辩护；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年人权律师浦志强被中共当局抓捕时，曾为其备选辩护人之一；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因其为北京传知行社会经济研究所负责人郭玉闪被捕案担任辩护人而被北京市警方突然从家中带走，随后被以涉嫌“赌博”和“诈骗”罪刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日又被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日其案被移送检察院审查起诉，但因证据不足曾被延期三次；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被该法院经一审以“诈骗罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万元。其不服上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经北京第二中级法院二审改判为有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前仍被关押在北京市第一看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，余光河突然被重庆市九龙坡区国保警察抓走，家被查抄，后得知因宣传法轮功信息被以涉邪教罪刑拘，关押在九龙坡区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日其被重庆市九龙坡区法院开庭受审，并被一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。其不服判决，立即提出上诉，但二审仍然维持原判。目前在重庆市永川监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆北碚区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，在北碚区居民住宅小区几处出现法轮功真相粘贴，当地警察怀疑是由袁志强提供，另一女性法轮功学员粘贴的。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，北碚区国保支队警察，闯进袁志强位于北碚区东阳街道磨心坡村的家中，抄走了大法书籍、真相数据和计算机、打印机等物品。袁志强被关押在北碚区三溪口看守所。后得知，袁志强被江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赞查（藏）、</span></span></span></span><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达日（藏）都是四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">33/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b 0pt;">张瑞君：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东淄博市法轮功学员。五十多岁，新华书店退休职工，家住淄博市高新区四宝山镇。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年三月十九日左右，张瑞君被淄博市桓台县国保跨区抓捕，被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，桓台县国保对她拘留、查体，并批捕。警察强迫家人给张瑞君办健康码后，在体检不合格的情况下，将她关押在淄博市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张瑞君被二次开庭，是视频开庭。在视频中，家人看到她已被迫害得非常严重。原本身体健康的她，说话时，反应迟钝，精神萎靡不振，走路都成问题。她的孩子了解到张瑞君睡眠、吃饭都相当差。由于体检有传染病，她被单独关押在一间屋里，不与任何人接触、说话。第二次开庭后，张瑞君被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。她不服判决，继续上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，家属得知，她已被送入济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/14/%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E5%BC%A0%E7%91%9E%E5%90%9B%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E5%A5%B3%E5%AD%90%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-440043.html"><span _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张英玲：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市凌海市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，锦州市公安局太和分局国保大队共抓捕了十几名法轮功学员，包括：张英玲（<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁）、金晓梅（<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁）、康桂云（<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁）、刘玉荣（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、李淑芳（<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁）、陈文学（<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁），都是老太太。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日获悉，辽宁省锦州市凌海市法院对这名老人下达判决，其中张英玲、金晓梅都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；康桂云<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；刘玉荣、李淑芳、陈文学皆被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金两千元。张英玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵恒德：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁夏法轮功学员。生于<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，原系宁夏隆德县卫生局干部，近几年居住在宁夏银川市。赵恒德<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上，发放法轮功资料，被警察抓捕。在当天晚上十点左右，警察到他家抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，赵恒德被银川市公安局兴庆区分局刑拘，关押在银川市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，赵恒德被逮捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，他被银川市公安局兴庆区分局警察构陷到银川市西夏区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，赵恒德在银川市西夏区法院被开庭。北京维权律师为他做了有理有据的无罪辩护，要求无罪释放。后被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，至今他被关押在银川市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周艳波：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，周艳波毕业于大连医科大学附属卫校，由国家统一分配到大连开发区医院工作，从事临床护理工作。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年，周艳波开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，没有经过任何法律程序，周艳波被劫持到了马三家劳教所，被劳教两年。遭酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被国保警察抓捕后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被视频非法开庭，周艳波被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前，周艳波仍被非法关押在大连姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">又名丁发栋，宁夏银川市法轮功学员丁乾，男，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，现年六十三岁。原系宁夏青铜峡市一所中学的优秀教师，还是宁夏优秀键盘手，他的音乐作品在全国首届中音杯获奖。早年修炼法轮功，一九九九年“七·二零”法轮功遭迫害后，丁乾曾四次被中共非法劳教，曾遭受过关禁闭、坐老虎凳、毒打等酷刑折磨，身陷囹圄逾八年。丁乾<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被青铜峡市公安局警察抓捕，关押在吴忠市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号，丁乾被批捕，后遭起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，其已被吴忠市利通区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金五千元，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月下旬被转监到宁夏石嘴山监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河北泊头市法轮功学员，家住河北省沧州泊头市寺门村镇韩集村。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午九时许，他在本村的工厂上班期间，被泊头市公安局抓捕。随即段志生被关押在泊头市看守所，数日后，他被转至任丘市看守所。后其遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，当地法院在看守所秘密开庭，没有通知家属，在家属不知道的情况下，段志生被判刑<span Roman&quot;;">那粉琼：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日生，开远罗白道旧寨社区小乐居民小组农民。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日法轮功学员张红英、那粉琼在另一法轮功学员家读《转法轮》时，被开远市公安国保警察抓捕。警察随后抄了张红英、那粉琼的家。随后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，那粉琼被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1500</span>元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/1.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/1.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">40/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王刚：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1958</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，河北省人，原河北工程大学临床医学院副教授，人类党网站（或人类党论坛）作者<span lang="EN-US">, </span>笔名“诺亚方舟”，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。十几年前，曾因发表多篇评论时政及反思文革的文章，而被其任职大学所在地河北省邯郸市当局视为重点监控对像；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，又因质疑中共享人制度及专制腐败现像等，发表《致中共中央的公开信》，呼吁政治改革，而被邯郸市丛台区警方贴身监控；后因其不惧危险，仍旧经常在微信上发表批评政府的文章，而曾被邯郸市警方处治安拘留<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次（第一次拘留<span lang="EN-US">19</span>天，第二次拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天），被喝茶<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多次；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因再次呼吁中共反腐和政改等，后又于同年创立“上海百姓维权”与“中国百姓维权”等微信群，表明中共绝不会走民主宪政之路，故而呼吁“民众移民”，但此言行被警方获悉，遂立遭丛台区联西派出所警方的野蛮执法，并派专人以“科研助手”名义对其进行贴身监视；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，“六四”来临前夕，其频遭当地警方约谈和做笔录，并被威胁称，若其尽快退出微信群，且不再在网上发表违规言论，就不对其翻旧账，但若继续发声，不仅会被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10-15</span>天，更会将其以前的案子推翻，再以“颠覆国家政权罪”论处；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其突遭警方立案侦查，并由公安部统一部署，在全国五六个省份（如闽、粤、湘和海南等省） 对其展开调查；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被邯郸市丛台区丛西派出所警方以约谈之名诱骗至派出所后失联，至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉，其已被邯郸市丛台区警方正式刑事拘留。目前被羁押于邯郸市第一看守所。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2022</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉：因言获罪六四前遭中共当局以刑事拘留的原河北工程大学临床医学院副教授王刚涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日由邯郸市公安局移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被中共当局以煽动颠覆国家政权罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前在河北邢台监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/26_27.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">41/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">易惠军：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南株洲民主人士，中国公民党代理总裁<span lang="EN-US">,1966</span>年生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>湖南株洲人。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，湖南株洲民主人士易惠军发布了《中国公民党宣言》，<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日当地警方闻讯到他家来找他，今天其多位朋友给其打电话，已无人接听，大概率已被抓捕。易惠军在其撰写的《中国公民党宣言》中写到：“<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日是中国公民党宣布成立之日！ 易惠军任首任中国公民党代理总裁。”“中国公民党的目标是：达成中国免费教育、免费医疗、免费养老，取消退休双轨制，人人平等。实行一人一票，两院制、三权分立。多党竞选上岗执政。将所有机构的党委彻底剥离，减轻纳税人负担。”该宣言最后写道：“天下苦秦久矣！这句活用在<span lang="EN-US">CCP</span>（中共）统治下的中国实在恰如其分。一党执政七十多年实在乏善可陈，就连体制内的前总理温家宝都强烈呼吁政治体制改革。 本党就是在这种环境下应运而生。公民党是一位共产党员提议，他解释道是每个人都能够被公平的对待。可见共产党内也有许多人怨声载道。宣言还强调说：本党旨在参政论政造福人民，请现任执政党不要将颠覆国家政权罪扣在本党头上。国家依旧在，只是独裁亡！<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>中国公民党总裁：易惠军<span lang="EN-US">2024.10.14 </span>左手书。”其被关押<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/blog-post_48.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span
