<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">42/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183699481"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姚静娇</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183699481;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东省揭阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年生，现年已<span lang="EN-US">85</span>岁高龄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，她在同村法轮功学员钟佩珍家中参加集体阅读《转法轮》一书时，被揭阳市公安局抓捕。姚静娇被关押一天后，以“取保候审”形式回家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金三万元。姚静娇老人于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被榕城区国保抓捕至揭东区看守所收监，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初又被转监至广东女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夜，广东女子监狱医院的救护车将姚静娇女士送到广东揭阳市中医院门口，<span lang="EN-US">85</span>岁的姚静娇外形已严重脱相，张大着嘴，不能说话，两只无神的眼睛尚能动。来接她的家属几乎认不出来。随车的狱警说，姚静娇右腿骨折合并多器官衰竭，生命危在旦夕，现交还家属。姚静娇老人随即被家属送往揭阳市中医院重症监护室抢救。据悉，出狱前，狱方先后三次向家属勒索三万元，否则不让出狱就医。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><a name="_Hlk170538828"></a><a name="_Hlk162565472"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b></span></a></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">毛孟静、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">全世欣、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">戴耀廷：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1964</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，英语名<span lang="EN-US">Benny Tai Yiu-ting</span>，原英属香港籍人，现中华人民共和国（香港）籍和英国籍人，基督徒，香港法律学者，前香港大学法律学院副院长和副教授，中共眼里的乱港“搞手”，“占中三子”，民主派意见领袖，中国在押政治犯。自幼生长于香港；<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代，中学毕业后曾就读于香港大学法律系，获取法律学士学位后，又取得法律深造证书，并在英国伦敦大学获得法律硕士学位；早年曾有浓烈的“中国情怀”，喜读中文和中国历史，后在大学期间，因吸收民主自由思想而认识到一国之强大不只是富国强兵，而是让它走向宪政，遂开始致力于研究宪法、宪政、公法、法律、政治和宗教的关系，人权及参与式民主等内容，并成为民主派意见领袖；大学毕业后，曾在民主派领袖李柱铭办公担任法案助理，并是《香港基本法咨询委员会》两位学生代表之一，同时对“一国两制”的实施提出了批判与质疑；之后曾多年在香港大学法律系当副教授、并曾在<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2008</span>年期间担任法律学院副院长；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾因提出“让爱与和平占领中环”观念而闻名；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因先后提出雷动计划、风云计划及民主派<span lang="EN-US">35+</span>初选等行动，而赢得香港市民的大力支持和响应，但却屡遭亲共建制派人士及媒体攻击。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因国安法在香港正式实施，其很快遭国安警方拘捕，罪由为曾发起占中运动，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月在香港中环金钟不同地点有“煽惑他人”或“煽惑他人煽惑”等行为；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被西九龙裁判法院庭审裁决「共谋犯公众妨扰」及「煽惑他人犯公众妨扰」罪名成立，并于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被判监<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个月；其不服上诉，并申请保释；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，服刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，终被获准以<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万港元保释等候上诉，但要求交出旅游证件，不可离港；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其保释被香港高级法院撤回而返监；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其再次因国安法规定下的涉嫌「串谋颠覆国家政权罪」而与其他<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年立法会选举民主派初选参与者（共<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人，后称<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人案）一起被捕；续押四年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人案中<span lang="EN-US">45</span>人被西九龙裁判法院裁定罪成，并指其与区诺轩、赵家贤、钟锦麟、吴政亨<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人是初选组织者，应被视为首要分子；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人在西九龙裁判法院被统一宣判，其中，其被判囚<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年监禁，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月；其余人等亦被重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月—<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月不等。目前在香港大屿山石壁监狱服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/10_20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/10_20.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-ascii-font-family: 等线; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 等线; mso-hansi-font-family: 等线;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王一飞：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1985</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，湖南省籍人士，化名小李，原网络秘密组织“兴中会”成员，网络秘密民运组织“兴华会”创建者和主要推动者，政治犯。多年来一直低调并积极从事民主运动，因创建并与异议人士曾国凡等多人积极推动网络组织“兴华会”，倡导国内民众成立公民圈，开展启发民智的行动，而深受江西当局严控打压；因该会成员及支持者在南昌、赣州等地多处建筑物上喷涂“官员财产公开，人民代表直选”、“平反八九六四，结束一党专政”、“六四英灵，永远安息”等官方敏感标语，其宣传标语落款为“兴华会”，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其与曾国凡夫妇随被南昌市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”悉数带走、刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被南昌市警方以同罪由正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年某日，被江西省南昌市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，刑满释放。此前在江西南昌市洪都监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月再遭抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日获悉王一飞被四川省泸州市法院判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前羁押在泸州市看守所一监区。目前罪名不详。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/76_16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/76_16.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><a name="_Hlk183684440"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></a></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183684440;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余慧明</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">简历：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，英文名：<span lang="EN-US">Winnie,YuWai Ming</span>，原英属香港籍、现中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，前香港医管局医疗信息部助理行政主任，前香港医管局内科护士、深切治疗部护士，前香港医管局总部<span lang="EN-US">IT</span>部职员，香港医管局员工阵线主席，泛民主派人士，民主派初选案（又称“<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案”）被告之一，在押政治犯。早年曾就读于香港中文大学医学院护理系；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2014</span>年，曾在香港医管局任职内科护士，后又转到深切治疗部任职；并曾言“不理世事”和时事；但自从<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年香港占领行动（又称“雨伞运动”）以来，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日香港政府向抗议市民投下了催泪弹，其开始意识到关心社会时政的必要性；后又因<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年香港《逃犯条例》修订引发了百万人大游行，再次促其对社会议题更多关注，随毅然与其他医护人员筹组工会，并出任工会组织主席；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾因不满医管局管理层无视在改用电子派药系统时出现漏洞而使其同事被迫辞职，以及系统人手不足等问题，而申请调职到总部的<span lang="EN-US">IT</span>部任职，以期了解改良一个电子系统的难度，从而更好地在体制中推动改革；曾因<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年冠状病毒疫情在香港蔓延，进而引发相关医护事宜的争议，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，其随发起医护人员大罢工，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又代表卫生服务界参与立法会民主派初选（官方又称“<span lang="EN-US">35+</span>初选”）；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其与<span lang="EN-US">40</span>余名泛民主派人士统一被香港国安处警方以涉嫌“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”拘捕；被控此前因参选立法会民主派区域选举，故而触犯了香港国安法规定；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其又被香港高等法院批准保释，但至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，因其保释期间在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>（脸书）上发布帖文，被香港当局认为危害国家安全及违反法院的保释条件，遂再次在香港沙田区被拘捕，次日即被西九龙裁判法院撤销保释，要求其再押侯审；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其因不认罪和求情信是「政治宣言，不见减刑因素」而被西九龙裁判法院裁定「串谋颠覆国家政权」罪成；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，终被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期预估至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。目前被羁押于荔枝角收押所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/69_24.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/69_24.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">伍健伟简历：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1995</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，英语名：<span lang="EN-US">Ng Kin-wai</span>，外号“<span lang="EN-US">K</span>先生”、<span lang="EN-US">Mr.K</span>，原英属香港籍人，现中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，香港新界元朗区公民，前银行业职员，“天水联机”（属政治党派）主要组建人，前元朗区议会议员，中共眼中的“港独”分子，民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾在香港新界元朗区长大；大学毕业后，曾在银行业任职，并曾积极参与雨伞革命和“反送中”抗议活动（即反对《逃犯条例修订草案》运动）；后因元朗袭击事件，其认为亲中派议员垄断区议会，在重大议题上并未传递民间声音，故而联合多名于网上平台上认识的天水围居民组成政治党派“天水联机”，准备出战<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年香港立法会区议会选举；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，其以“天水联机”成员身份正式宣布并参选嘉湖北选区议会选举；期间，曾因和其他民主派元朗区候选人均有合作，故当民主党立法会议员、元朗区议员邝俊宇于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭歹徒伏击，遇袭受伤后，其立即与多名其他民主派人士共同联署谴责警方执法不公，要求港警公平执法；后经区议会选举激烈角逐，其最终击败原任亲中派议员李月民等参选人而胜出，并于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日正式任职；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因参与元朗袭击事件半周年集会之时，在元朗港铁站进行放映会叫市民毋忘事件之后，有大批防暴警察以查案为由前来围堵和抓捕与警方发生冲突的市民聚集者，其在现场劝架时，不幸遭警方胡椒喷雾喷中，并与天水联机”成员林进等共<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人一起被以涉嫌“组织未经批准集结罪”拘留；后其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人很快被释放，但再之后又被中共港府列为<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案之一，被香港国安处警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案被国安处警方指控涉嫌“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”，且大部分被告申请保释经香港高级法院<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天复核后，最终法官仅批准其中<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人以极严苛的条件予以保释，而其之申请被拒；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其与同党人林进在所属区的屯门裁判法院又被追加指控为“组织受禁群组聚集罪”，二人认罪被判罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天之后，其被辞任区议员职务；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其再次向香港高级法院申请保释，但再次遭拒，并被指仍须续押候审；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其等「<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选颠覆罪」案成员在西九龙裁判法院宣判，因其多次审判称“无悔”，不为信仰与价值观道歉，遂被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，刑期预至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前被羁押于荔枝角收押所。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/57_25.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/57_25.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">5/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄之锋：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1996</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Joshua Wong Chi-fung</span>，基督徒，国籍中国（香港）、英国国民，无党籍民主派人士，荣获美国《时代杂志》<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年度<span lang="EN-US">25</span>名最具影响力少年之一之称， “雨伞运动”领军者，香港学运思潮召集人、香港众志秘书长，中国在押政治犯。自幼曾随父母参与教会活动，做义工，热心服务于小区公共事务；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾就读香港公开大学，并于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月以优异成绩从大学毕业；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，曾与中学校友林朗彦成立学生组织“学民思潮”，曾多次组织学生游行、集会等，以反对香港政府假借德育及国民教育科向学生进行拥护中国共产党的洗脑教育，从而引起社会各界广泛关注；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾受邀出席《城市论坛》，就国民教育议题与其他嘉宾辩论，因表现出色而获公众广泛赞许，并成为全香港反对「洗脑教育」运动全面爆发的导火线；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，曾因参与雨伞运动，主导学生举行「和平占中」罢课集会而被警方拘捕，后被取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因与林朗彦等人成立香港众志，提倡香港自治，不主张香港独立，同时表明「如无民主自治，只能选择港独」，而成为“不合北京心意的人”；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，曾因重夺公民广场事件而再度被捕，被香港高等法院以“非法集会罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，又被法院以「刑事藐视法庭罪」加获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被减刑至<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；出狱后，因又加入「反送中」运动，显示政府应明确撤回逃犯条例修订草案及撤回<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日百万人大游行定性为暴动的错误，同时指林郑月娥因造成香港人流血而已无资格再当特首，故使港府及中共当局更加不安；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，香港国际机场爆发大规模集结示威在即，因其在脸书上做直播<span lang="EN-US">,</span>呼吁届时游行人数能越百万等，随被警方于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在街头带走，并被检方指控涉嫌「煽惑他人参与未经批准的集结」等罪；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因准备前往德国讨论香港情况而又被警方以「违反保释条件」罪由拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，曾因报名参选区议会选举，而被北京的「硬命令」剥夺参选权；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾因中国人大通过《港版国安法》，而被迫宣布辞去香港众志秘书长一职，同时退出香港众志，表明其将在今后以个人身份实践信念；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，因包围香港警察总部案件，其与周庭和林朗彦一同被警方再度关押，期间虽暂获取保，但之后又被收监逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其三人案在香港西九龙法院被以「煽惑他人参与未经批准集结「组织未经批准集结」、「明知而参与未经批准集结」三罪开庭受审，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被分别宣判，其中，其被获刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>个半月<span lang="EN-US">;</span>早前曾因<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日的铜锣湾非法集结案已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年又因涉及“六四”烛光晚会“未经批准集结”案而再被香港区域法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，经上诉后缩减为<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，且前后两次获刑的刑期分别执行。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其服刑完毕，但因之前参与<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年立法会初选之事又遭指控，称其行为违反了港区国安法「颠覆国家政权罪」，遂仍须关在赤柱监狱等候续审<span lang="EN-US">; 2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因被指控「泄露警员个人资料」，而被香港高等法院以「藐视法庭罪」判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">;2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人颠覆罪案在西九龙裁判法院统一宣判，被以「串谋颠覆国家政权罪」判囚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月监禁，刑期预至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。目前在香港赤柱监狱服刑。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family: 等线; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 等线; mso-hansi-font-family: 等线;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/48.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/48.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></u></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毛孟静<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女<span lang="EN-US">,1957</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，祖籍浙江省宁波市，中英双国籍香港人，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Claudia Mo Man-ching</span>，昵称：毛姨姨、连登契妈、毛姑姑、毛婆，基督徒，香港资深传媒人，香港中文大学政治与行政学系讲师（兼任），香港公民党、民主党联合创办人，香港特别行政区立法会议员，香港民主派会议召集人，中国在押政治犯。自幼生长在香港；中学毕业后曾到加拿大安大略省留学，并于<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年在渥太华卡尔顿大学新闻系（副修英国文学）毕业；回港后，曾分别在法新社和《英文虎报》担任法文及英文记者，又在香港无线电视新闻部担任主播及在香港电台担任节目主持等；<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代，曾长期担任六点半新闻报道主播，亦担任香港电台电视节目《城市论坛》现场直播节目主持、《传媒春秋》节目主持以及有线电视儿童台节目主持等；曾在香港浸会大学新闻系和香港中文大学政治与行政学系兼任讲师；曾为报纸撰写专栏评论，并在<span lang="EN-US">A45</span>网上电台担任唱片骑师；曾出版过多部书籍，并言曾在北京采访过“六四清场”，深有“接近死亡之感”<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾代表公民党参加这年香港立法会选举，最后成功当选；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，再次参选香港立法会选举，并以高票获成功连任；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因与公民党在本土等问题上有分歧，随正式退出公民党，而以香港本土成员身份担任立法会议员；因其政治立场被认为是相对较理解年轻人的主流民主派，即属于自治派和中间偏左，支持“本土主义”，强调“务实本土路线”，反对“香港大陆化”，反对改用大陆用语，认同香港人应有“自决权”，但不支持港独和以武力方式应对“中港矛盾”等，故被中共当局视为需要重拳打击的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，香港国家安全法（简称国安法）正式生效，其等数十人因参与<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年香港立法会选举九龙西民主派初选，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，遂与其他参选成员共计<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人被香港警方统一以违反国安法条例规定抓捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人案被九龙西法院正式指控为“串谋颠覆国家政权”罪成；后其向香港高等法院申请保释遭拒，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在西九龙法院再度提审，告知其等多人仍须续押待审；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人颠覆罪案在西九龙裁判法院统一宣判，多人被重判，其中，其被判囚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期预估至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前被羁押于香港荔枝角收押所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源<u>：</u></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/42_23.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/42_23.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><a name="_Hlk183693322"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></a></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183693322;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">全世欣：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183693322;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，北京市人，北京市海淀区四季青东平庄<span lang="EN-US">56</span>号居民，维权人士，贪腐举报人，网络推友。早年曾因个人宅基地及住房被政府强拆而被迫维权多年，至今仍未获批宅基地或获赔住房，成为无家可归的北京土著农民；在维权过程中，因发现地方干部有严重贪腐现象，并公开向多个职能部门举报，随遭地方当权者严厉打压和非法拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，因使用互联网翻墙软件在推特上发表对中共当局及执政者批评言论，被网警监控发现，而被北京海淀区警方因言获罪，立刻以“寻衅滋事”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因身穿写有“蔡奇见家属”字样的白色短袖<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤，高喊要求与市政府相关负责人见面递交相关材料，寻求解决问题，而被海淀区警方以“扰乱公共场所秩序”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，再次被海淀区警方莫名带走，后被以“寻衅滋事”罪由刑拘，好友疑称此与其曾在推特上多次发支持香港“反送中”抗议游行等言论有关；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其被起诉，起诉书称其“自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年注册并使用推特，散布大量虚假信息，严重扰乱社会秩序”，因而触犯刑法，需要提交法院予以审判；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在北京市海淀区法院开庭受理，后又长期休庭；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，刑满释放。此前被羁押于北京市海淀区看守所。全世欣女士<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日就两会被维稳监控接受了美国之音采访，随即遭抓捕，其推特账号停留在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。后被刑事拘留、批捕，已被检察院起诉，建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其身患心脏病，现在又绝食抗争，其狱中健康令人担忧。最后全世欣女士一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月 二审维持原判。现被羁押于北京市海淀区看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183693322;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳、张展、卢思位、陆辉煌、黄雪琴、王建兵、张晓东、吴孔大、季孝龙等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人狱中动态信息通报：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳：湖南人权律师谢阳狱中通讯权被剥夺<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，本网获悉：湖南人权律师谢阳被关押超过<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，至今仍未开庭。日前其通讯权被剥夺。陈桂秋女士今日通报：“谢阳律师通讯权被剥夺。我于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日邮寄了一封信给谢阳，但是信件被拒收。现在终于有证据证明他的通讯权被剥夺了。这快三年的时间里，他的家人和我的家人从来没有收到过他邮寄的任何信件，我这次邮寄给他的信件，被长沙市看守所拒绝接收。现在的长沙市第一看守所的所长是谁？请网友帮忙寻找他的个人信息，谢谢。以前的所长李源，貌似被撤职了。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳律师简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，湖南省长沙市人，天地人律师事务所和长沙京盈科律师事务所前任律师，原湖南纲维律师事务所律师，人权律师，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年正式执业以来，曾因代理多起公权力滥权案件，如山东省曲阜县薛明凯案、北京新公民运动张宝成案、河南省南乐县南乐教案、湖南省浏阳市张开华征地案等维权案件，并积极关注和参与社会维权运动（包括探访盲人律师陈光诚和声援建三江被捕律师等），而屡遭司法当局阻扰和逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾因只身前往山东省东师古村探望盲人律师陈光陈，而被地方黑恶势力殴打抢劫；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因代理一起民间借贷纠纷案，为维护当事人利益要求取得合议庭商议结果，而被湖南省律师协会罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，并被所在事务所要求解除合同和离职；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因为“山东薛家命案”作委托代理律师，而被湖南省司法厅当局带走“约谈喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因为代理湖南省浏阳市土地维权者张开华案，在出庭时遭到当地法院的野蛮阻扰；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因多次代理维权案件，而遭到湖南省律师协会变相打压，不予批准转所手续；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因其积极代理多起长沙市雨花区强制征地拆迁案件，在代理莲湖村农民征地行政诉讼时，曾遭到当地法院非法驱逐；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其代理广西南宁北部湾建材市场当事人的维权案件，曾遭到多名不明身份人员的持械群殴，致其重伤，右腿骨折，其虽报警，但当地警方却迟迟不予出警；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其在中共“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>大逮捕”中被湖南省长沙市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“扰乱法庭秩序”、“煽动颠覆国家政权”二罪指定地点监视居住，代理律师要求会见遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案在湖南省长沙中级法院开庭受审，但因其被迫当庭认罪，否认曾受酷刑，遂于当日暂获取保候审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市中级法院正式宣判：犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，但免予刑事处罚；后其虽未被判刑入狱，但仍遭长期软禁和贴身监控；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，谢阳因<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年末前往湖南省永顺县声援因发表网络言论而被强制关进精神病院的怀孕女教师李田田，遂被长沙市警方带走失联，后知被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；其住处遭查抄，许多个人物品均被损毁，两台计算机及一个保险柜被搜走；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被长沙市检察院以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”予以正式批捕。狱中遭酷刑。谢阳案是大陆人权捍卫者被迫害的缩影，他自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年以来多次被拘押；谢阳在狱中经历了难以想象的酷刑、虐待和羞辱，案件被当局故意<span lang="EN-US">9</span>次延期，狱中被剥夺通信权，以此对谢阳及其家人施加精神折磨。目前谢阳律师被羁押于长沙市第一看守所（湖南省长沙市长沙县泉塘街道远大二<span lang="EN-US">1736</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">410131</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/blog-post_35.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/blog-post_35.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展：著名人权捍卫者张展女士日前被正式批捕<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，本网获悉：已遭羁押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月的著名人权捍卫者张展女士日前遭正式批捕。经浦东新区检察院批准，上海市公安局浦东分局于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪对张展女士执行逮捕。目前张展被羁押在浦东新区看守所。张展女士曾获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月才刑满出狱。出狱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月后，即<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，张展因营救被抓捕的甘肃青年民主活动人士张盼成，从上海只身赴甘肃，说服张母签署了委托书。后其回到老家陕西咸阳，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在当地被上海警方带回上海，后遭当局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，目前已经被批捕。张展被抓捕后，引起国际社会的高度关注。当局仍然以各种方式封锁张展案的信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，陕西省咸阳市人，上海市浦东新区居民，曾任职于上海市某证券公司高管，原执业律师，公民记者，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早期，曾就读于西南财经大学金融专业并获取硕士学位；自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，离开家乡到上海谋职；曾为追求自由理想而甘愿放弃在一家证券公司的高薪职位；曾任职律师，但后因在网上发表针砭时弊的文章而遭报复，被迫离开律师岗位；因不满中共当局的政治现状，曾长期在网络平台发表批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，且因内容尖锐，颇具针对性，而被上海警方多次约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因在微信等社交软件上大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是在上海街头举伞要求结束社会主义制度、共产党下台等，随于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海市黄浦区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，期间曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”，至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日才准予取保候审释放；自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年初以来，曾因武汉冠状病毒疫情蔓延，其为了获取一手数据，不惧风险，亲赴武汉做实地疫情考察与报导；此举很快遭到中共当局的极端不满和迅速打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被武汉警方从一家暂住旅店抓走，次日被上海市浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被浦东新区检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其案被移送至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日；据悉，其家属要求探监曾长期遭拒；其因狱中长期绝食抗议，被强行灌食，致其身体情况十分虚弱。此前张展一直在上海市女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因赴甘肃营救张盼成，再遭当局抓捕，被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被正式批捕。目前羁押在浦东看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/blog-post_26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/blog-post_26.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢思位：卢思位最新情况的通报（<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春晓（卢思位妻子）：原订<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日的庭前会<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被通知改期，原因是承办法官突发疾病。律师前天下午会见了思位，他的健康状态令人担忧。银屑病的药一直没有到位，便秘严重。几年前做过甲状腺手术，最近检查了一下甲状腺，出现甲亢症状。生活条件很差！现在每天的工作是接水，早晨要打扫外监室的收纳箱，每两天值班一次。平时就坐着，两个穿绿马甲的人包夹他，他被列为三级风险人员。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢思位：<span lang="EN-US">1</span></span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">973</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，四川省知名人权律师，办理过成都纪念「八九六四」酒案，是成都「四君子」之一张隽勇的辩护人，曾代理十二港人“偷渡案”、余文生 、王藏 、覃永沛 、陈家鸿 等“煽动颠覆国家政权案”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，卢思位律师就发起公民联署，呼吁全国人大成立特别调查委员会，就“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>”系列案件是否存在强迫服药等酷刑进行独立调查，调查委员会的组成人员应当包括律师和公民代表，并向公开调查结论。厦门聚会案发生后，卢思位律师受到传唤及威胁，并被禁止出境。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日卢思位律师因办理过广西律师陈家鸿「煽动颠覆国家政权案」，曾遭受四川司法当局和律师协会打压和处分。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，余文生律师因煽动颠覆国家政权罪成，被徐州市中级法院判处徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，卢思位律师作为二审辩护人参与辩护工作。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，有十二位香港社运人士被深圳公安扣押在盐田看守所，卢思位律师曾经探访十二位被扣押香港人，又向他们提供法律援助。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日成都市羊青区司法局对卢思位律师代理的所有案件材料检查。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，四川省司法厅对卢思位律师开出行政处罚案件当事人听证权利告知书，准备吊销卢律师的律师执业证。后卢思位遭吊销律师证。卢思位先生于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午在准备登上一列开往泰国的火车时，被老挝警方逮捕。卢思位的原定行程是在泰国搭乘班机前往美国与家人团聚。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月卢思位被老挝政府连同其他<span lang="EN-US">50</span>名中国人，一起分乘两辆车，遣返中国。随后，卢思位被中共当局关押到四川成都市新都看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，卢思位律师取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，卢思位被传唤到保和派出所做了三个小时左右的笔录，随后被告知，他的案子将由成华区公安局移送成华区检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其再遭抓捕。目前羁押于成都看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/20241122.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/20241122.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk183690353"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陆辉煌</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的广西民主人士陆辉煌目前关押在广西钦州监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的广西民主人士陆辉煌目前关押在广西钦州监狱服刑，通信地址：广西壮族自治区钦州市钦北区北营路<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号，邮编<span lang="EN-US">: 535099</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陆辉煌：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">男，壮族，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，户籍所在地：广西贵港市桂平市垌心乡上瑶村方和屯<span lang="EN-US">94</span>号。曾在广东珠三角等地工作，工作之余关心国家、民生状况，进行写作并在网络上传播。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 10 </span>月，其写了《致中共中央公开信——关于政治体制改革的思考和建议》，在文中分析了国家的政治体制并建议中共中央进行宪政改革<span lang="EN-US">2016 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>月，其写了《“妄议”国事》一文，在文中批评了个别国家领导人和政策。<span lang="EN-US">2016 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 6 </span>月，其写下《致习近平总书记的公开信》，呼吁习近平关注、关心农民工。以上三篇文章只是在一些<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群和一些<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>好友中传播。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1 </span>月，其写了《对当前政局的分析与呼吁》，在文中分析了当时的时局，反对修宪和个人崇拜，并通过<span lang="EN-US"> QQ </span>、微信、邮箱传播，并向《北京之春》网站投稿，《北京之春》网站分别于<span lang="EN-US"> 2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 2 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">25 </span>日和<span lang="EN-US"> 2 </span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 28 </span>日分上篇和下篇刊登了该文。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 7 </span>月，其写作《“艰时克共”的建议》，呼吁早日促进《零八宪章》的目标实现，并通过微信群传播，后又在《北京之春》网站刊登。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 7</span>月，其写了《致“中国劳工观察”组织的信》，在文中描述了中国劳工特别是农民工的真实情况，并请求“中国劳工观察”组织帮助他们维权，并通过<span lang="EN-US"> QQ </span>、微信，向朋友传播。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其在深圳富士康鸿观厂区被深圳市龙华区公安分局福民派出所传唤到该派出所。（<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在签刑事拘留通知书时，其知道并没有人报案，他们是根据上级部门监控发现深圳有人传播所谓政治不当言论的线索，并依据文章的线索传唤。）在派出所里，警察在还没立案（也就是说还没进入刑事阶段）之前，就利用威胁（不说就打）手段获取其手机、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱等密码，并利用这些密码非法登录其<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱，搜集其所谓犯罪证据。就这样，公安机关在其手机便签、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱搜集到了前面其所列举的六篇文章。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，公安机关以这六篇文章作为证据开始立案，将其刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日将其逮捕，之后经过两次退回补充侦查，三次延长审查起诉。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2019</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，深圳市龙华检察院以所谓的散布虚假信息、辱骂国家领导人、造谣污蔑国家的政治体制、法律制度、基本国策、指导思想、战略布局、反腐斗争、发展路线、劳工制度与现状、民族复兴目标等，涉嫌寻衅滋事罪起诉，所谓的罪证就是其前面列举的六篇文章。由于其坚持不认罪，并在里面坚持斗争，遭遇了杨伟东恶警施加的电击、禁食、戴镣铐等酷刑。并且不准其与家人通信。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日（接到起诉书的第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天），在深圳市龙华法院开庭前会议，就证据的合法性进行质疑。由于家人没有给其请律师，其律师是官派的，在这次庭前会议上根本没有就证据的合法性为其辩护。而陆辉煌本人就检方的证据提出三个疑点：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、其写的文章属于言论自由的范畴。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、检方的证据是利用非法手段（威胁手段）取得的。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、检方指控其在《北京之春》刊发文章，也是通过翻墙的手段获得的，根据《宪法》人人平等的原则，公检法等机关并没有特权，他们能用的，咱们平民百姓也能用。他们能翻墙，咱平民百姓也能翻墙，那就没有必要浪费大量纳税人的钱去建所谓的“防火墙”了。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，在深圳市龙华法院正式开庭。其本人写的辩护词不让其带到法庭。在上车去法庭时，法警给其戴上头套，只露出眼睛，到了法院才摘下来。在庭审时，审判长江涛以不准辱骂国家领导人为由阻止其为自己辩护。庭审只用了大约一个小时就草草结束。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其接到判决书，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，由于在看守所长期睡地板，导致其得了风湿，腰椎疾病。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被调往广东省从化监狱服刑，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日刑满释放。释放后多次申诉无果。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点，广西异议人士陆辉煌在南宁市大岭新村居住地被多名不明身份男子带走。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午，朋友拨打不通陆辉煌电话，致电陆辉煌户籍所在地广西贵港市桂平市垌心乡派出所询问，接线员否认有抓陆辉煌，但言语闪烁其词。陆辉煌曾因言论获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月刑满释放。有网友猜测陆辉煌被再次带走，或与其签名呼吁彻查徐州铁链女奴事件有关。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2022</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，陆辉煌被广西壮族自治区贵港市法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日；其不服，已表示上诉。此前其被羁押于广西贵港市看守所。目前转监在钦州监狱服刑，通信地址：广西壮族自治区钦州市钦北区北营路<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号，邮编<span lang="EN-US">: 535099</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/46_22.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/46_22.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/6/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄雪琴、王建兵：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年的著名人权捍卫者黄雪琴被转监广东省女子监狱获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的王建兵被转监至广东省阳春监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，本网获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，广东省高院对黄雪琴、王建兵突袭性秘密宣判，驳回两人的上诉。黄雪琴、王建兵两人于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日收到法院判决执行材料。近日获悉，两人已经于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日已经正式移送监狱服刑，其中，黄雪琴被转监至广东省女子监狱，王建兵被转监至广东省阳春监狱。两人移送监狱后的近况仍然无法得知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄雪琴简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1988</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，广东省韶关市人，女权独立记者，《新快报》及《南都周刊》前调查记者，性别、平权、官员贪污、企业污染和弱势群体等议题关注者，中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>运动重要支持者及<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>案件报导者，性侵害<span lang="EN-US">/</span>性骚扰受害人支持帮助者，女权活动家，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，即中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>元年以来，因其一直积极介入女权与<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>运动，并曾协助多名女性在网上举报性侵和性虐待案，随遭广东省当局的维稳监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因到香港参加“反送中”示威游行，且事后撰文公开分享感受，对港府严酷对待和平示威民众的强硬态度十分生气，随被广州市警方没收护照和港澳通行证；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，又曾以同理由，被广州警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后又被改为指定居所监视居住，直到<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，方得取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因其成功获得英国志奋领奖学金支持，将于次日前往萨塞克斯大学<span lang="EN-US">(University of Sussex)</span>就读性别与发展学硕士，突然与为其送行的公益人士王建兵一起失联，后知其二人均被广州市警方以“多次邀朋友在王建兵家中聚会，二人或有涉嫌组织有关时政类讨论活动之言行”为理由，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”拘留，后又被以同罪名转为指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被广州市警方以同罪名予以正式逮捕；因其及王建兵之名中的“雪”“兵”二字与“雪饼”谐音，故有支持者将其二人案又称为“雪饼”案，并在社交媒体上建立“雪饼案”专页，以及时、广泛关注其案信息；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其二人案历经<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久终于在广州市中级法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，二人被法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”同天庭审宣判：其被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，没收个人财产<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元；王建兵被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，没收个人财产<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；其二人不服，均提起上诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，经广东省高级法院二审裁决，其依然被维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日；据悉，其在被指定居所监视居住期间，曾遭刑讯逼供和长期疲劳审等非人道虐待，以致其身体严重出现损害和生理性紊乱。此前被羁押于广州市第一看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日黄雪琴被转监至广东省女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王建兵简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1983</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，甘肃省天水市人，化名“煎饼”，独立公益人，北京西部阳光基金会前农村教育项目主管，广州恭明社会组织发展中心前青少年成长项目主管和残障社群赋能项目统筹，职业病工人权益倡导者，法律知识指导服务者，中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>运动重要支持者，中国劳工行动者，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年大学毕业以来，热心从事公益事业<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年，故朋友及认识他的人都喜叫其「煎饼」；曾积极加入北京西部阳光农村发展基金从事农村发展工作，并担任该基金会农村教育项目主管<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；曾为开启长期关注青少年教育及成长的公益职业生涯，而于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年加入广州恭明社会组织发展中心，担任青少年成长项目和残障小区赋能项目主管及统筹，支持和发起相关小区项目工作；<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年起，开始关注职业病工人权益宣传及服务性工作，并提供必要的法律支持，同年，为关注和支持中国妇女人权活动，而成为中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>运动中重要的支持者；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其与其关系甚密的好友、独立记者黄雪琴同时失联，其租赁屋遭查抄；后经其父母家人及亲朋好友多方打探，知其二人均被广东省广州市警方以涉嫌「煽动颠覆国家政权罪「拘留，后又被指因其家中常有朋友聚会，恐有涉嫌组织有关时政类讨论的活动，故而被警方以同罪由指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被广州市警方以涉嫌」煽动颠覆国家政权罪」正式逮捕；因黄雪琴与其姓名中的“雪”、与「兵」二字和「雪饼」谐音，故而有支持者将其二人案称为「雪饼」案，并在社交媒体上建立「雪饼案」专页，以向众关注着及时广泛提供案情讯息；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其二人案历经<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久终于在广州市中级法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，两人被法院一审以「煽动颠覆国家政权罪」同天庭审宣判：黄雪琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，王建兵被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，没收个人财产<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；对此两人不服，均提起上诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，经广东省高等法院二审裁决，其仍被维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日；据悉，拘押审讯期间，曾遭刑讯逼供。此前被羁押于广州市第一看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日王建兵被转监至于广东省阳春监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size:
